<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подымать.html>подыма́вший</a> (7293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***подытожить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подытожить.html>подыто́жить</a> (17082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ито́жить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">itóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:итог.html>ито́г</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">itóg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подытожить.html>подыто́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podytóžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подыто́живать</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подыхать.html>подыха́ть</a> (18001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дыха́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dyxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подыхать.html>подыха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podyxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подохнуть.html>подо́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die, to croak, to kick the bucket</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подышать.html>подыша́ть</a> (10505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дышать.html>дыша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dyšátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>to breathe

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***поединок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поединок.html>поеди́нок</a> (6201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pojedynek</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">duel, rencounter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">po-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">jeden</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">-ek</i>. Cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единый.html>еди́ный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поединок.html>поеди́нок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojedínok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поединок.html>поеди́нка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поединок.html>поеди́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поединок.html>поеди́нков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>duel, rencounter</li>
<li>combat, fight, battle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́дом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поединок.html>поеди́нка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:боксер.html>боксёров</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязательно.html>обяза́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдать.html>наблюда́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:врач.html>врач</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Za xódom <b>pojedínka</b> boksjórov objazátelʹno nabljudájet vrač.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It's mandatory that a doctor observes the course of the boxers' fight.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dispute, quarrel, argument</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поеживаться.html>поёживаться</a> (17513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поеживаться.html>поёживаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojóživatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поеживаться.html>поёживаться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pojóživatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>

***поезд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>поезд</a> (830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pojazd</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/2M62M-1198_Kyviskes-Kena.jpg/220px-2M62M-1198_Kyviskes-Kena.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/2M62M-1198_Kyviskes-Kena.jpg/330px-2M62M-1198_Kyviskes-Kena.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/2M62M-1198_Kyviskes-Kena.jpg/440px-2M62M-1198_Kyviskes-Kena.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="804" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>поезд</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pójezd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>поезда́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>поездо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> caravan, convoy, procession</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> train, a line of connected railway cars
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езде</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jézditʹ na <b>pójezde</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go (or travel) by train</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скоростной.html>скоростно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skorostnój <b>pójezd</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">bullet train</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a method of fishing, in which a fishing net is pulled by two side-by-side boats</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a net used for this method of fishing</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поездка.html>пое́здка</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojézdka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поездно́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojezdnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***поездить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поездить.html>пое́здить</a> (24695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поездить.html>пое́здить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojézditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go (by horse or vehicle), to ride, to drive</li>
<li>to come, to visit</li>
<li>to travel</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поездить.html>пое́здить</a></b> is an abstract verb. Its counterparts, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.</li>
<li>All compounds of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></b> are formed from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>вы́езжать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výjezžatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поезжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pojezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приезжать.html>приезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.)</li></ul>

***поесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поесть.html>пое́сть</a> (3317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поесть.html>пое́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojéstʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поедать.html>поеда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to eat, to have a bite (of something to eat), to try (eat)</li></ol>

***поехать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a> (494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></b>) <i>(concrete)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to go <i>(in a conveyance or on horseback)</i></li>
<li>to ride, to drive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pojéxatʹ</b> za górod</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to go to the suburbs of a city by driving (suburbs are described as something "behind" a city)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to travel
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́ду</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чту</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>pojédu</b> na póčtu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm going to go to the post office. <i>(concrete)</i></span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>Пое́хать</a></b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a> are concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

***пожалеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалеть.html>пожале́ть</a> (2584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалеть.html>жале́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žalétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожалеть.html>пожале́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">požalétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалеть.html>жале́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to feel sorry, to be sorry, to be sad (about something), to regret</li>
<li>to pity, to commiserate</li>
<li>to save, to spare (e.g. time, energy)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожалеть.html>сожале́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sožalétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожаление.html>сожале́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sožalénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">жале́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žalénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***пожаловать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́ловать</a> (795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́ловать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žálovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́ловать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">požálovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́ловать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grant (to); to bestow, to confer (on); to reward, to award <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stilted style</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit, to come to see <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stilted style or jocular</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́ловал</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>каки́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьба́ми</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>су́дьбами</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kto k nam <b>požáloval</b>! Kakími sudʹbámi/súdʹbami?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Look who has come to <b>visit</b>! What brings you here?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́ловать</a></b>!</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">set expression</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dobró <b>požálovatʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Welcome!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to favour, to regard with favour; to like
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> о́чень-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́луют</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó ne óčenʹ-to <b>žálujut</b> tam.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is not very <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> there.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловаться.html>пожа́ловаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">požálovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловаться.html>жа́ловаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žálovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***пожалуйста.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a> (834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Lexicalization of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́луй</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">požáluj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ста</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an obsolete clitic that was used to add emphasis and to signify politeness, of obscure origin. The clitic is no longer used or known to most speakers, even as passive vocabulary, and has essentially disappeared from the language. Accordingly, to modern speakers, the ending of the word <i><a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a></i> is merely a sequence of sounds of indeterminate meaning.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">požálujsta</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>please
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da, <b>požálujsta</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Yes, <b>please</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>you're welcome, not at all, don't mention it, it's a pleasure (reply to thank you)</li>
<li>here you are (<i>when handing something over</i>)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожар.html>пожа́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">požár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожар.html>пожа́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожар.html>пожа́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожар.html>пожа́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fire, conflagration (occurrence of fire in a certain place)</li></ol>
